CREATE TABLE [dbo].[snap_Templates](
	[DocEntry] [INT] NOT NULL,
	[Dscpt] [VARCHAR](200) NULL,
	[WhsCode] [VARCHAR](3) NOT NULL,
	[RowNo] [INT] NULL,
	[CreateDate] [DATE] NULL,
	[EmpID] [VARCHAR](20) NULL,
	[TBType] [VARCHAR](2) NULL,
	[BegFormula] [VARCHAR](500) NULL,
	[CurrFormula] [VARCHAR](500) NULL,
	[EndFormula] [VARCHAR](500) NULL,
	[DscrptFS] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[AmtFS] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[DscrptFC] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[AmtFC] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[DscrptBG] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[AmtBG] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[DscrptTop] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[DscrptBot] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[AmtTop] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[AmtBot] [VARCHAR](30) NULL,
	[IsHidden] [INT] NULL,
	[IsMod] [INT] NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_snapTemplates] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[DocEntry] ASC,
	[WhsCode] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
